 Apart from Advani, several other leaders including Jaswant Singh, Yashwant Sinha, Uma Bharati and Shatrughan Sinha also did not attend the Goa meeting
 kaha ja rahaa he ki ye netaa modi kaa kad badhane se khush nahin hai
 After two days of ups and downs, ignoring the disagreement of leaders like Advani, the party seems to be giving a big and important role to Modi
 party main atal bihari vaajapeyi ke baad duusare number par adwani ko hi sabase bade kad kaa netaa mana jaataa rahaa he
 Rajnath said that all parties see the elections as a challenge and the BJP has also accepted the upcoming Lok Sabha elections as a challenge
 chunaavon main jeet hasil karne ke makasad se hi modi ko badi jimmedaari saunpi gai he
 Rajnath said, we are very confident that the Congress-led UPA government has lost the trust of the public and is also confident that the BJP will come to power by winning the 2014 elections
 varsh 2014 main hone vaale aam chunaav ke prachaar kii kaman modi ko saunpane kii ghoshnaa bhaajapa adhyaksh rajnath singh ne party kii do divasiy rashtriya kaaryakarini kii baithak ke antim din ek samvaadadaata sammelan main kii
 He was accompanied by senior party leaders Sushma Swaraj, Arun Jaitley and Anant Kumar
 rajnath ne samvaadadaataaon se kaha, "aane vaala loksabhaa chunaav ek badi chunauti he
 We are going to win
 chunaav abhiyaan ko dhyaan main rakhte hue maine narendra modi ko aam chunaav ke liye party kii prachaar samiti kaa pramukh niyukt kiya he
 " modi ko agle aam chunaav ke liye prachaar abhiyaan kii kaman saunpe jane ko lekar bhaajapa main antarvirodhon ko khaarij karte hue rajnath ne kaha, "yah nirnay sahmati se liya gaya he
 We are confident that the BJP will lead the next government
 " On the other hand, Modi is being offended by being made the head of the bjp's campaign committee and 'hurt' by the performance of Modi supporters outside his house
 Senior party leader LK Advani on Sunday took to his blog from historical characters like Hilter, Mussolini Referring to mythological characters like Bhishma Pitamah and warrior Arjuna, who were injured and victims of deception
 adwani ne apane blog par 'taanaashaahee pravriti' kaa bhi zikr kiya, jise aalochak modi ke swabhaav main dekhte hai
 Goa Chief Minister Manohar Parrikar also supported Modi

 Party workers started celebrating fiercely after the announcement of Modi being made the chairman of the election committee
 sutron ke mutabik party ne shanivaar ko hi rajya ikaayiyon ko nirdesh de diya tha ki jaise hi narendra modi ke naam kii ghoshnaa ho rajya karyaalayon main jashn kaa maahaul dikhaaya jaae
 Senior party leader LK Advani had agreed to make Narendra Modi the convener of the campaign committee on this issue, but Advani was not being persuaded to make Modi the chairman of this committee
 adwani tabiyat kharaab hone kaa hawala dete hue goa baithak main shaamil nahin hue the, lekin sutron ke mutabik adwani goa main na hokar bhi modi virdohi kheme kii kaman sanbhale hue the
 After being made the chairman of the campaign committee, Narendra Modi will preside over the bjp's meetings related to the election, but if Modi was made the convenor of the campaign committee, Rajnath Singh would have chaired the meetings for the election
 adwani ke alaava jaswant singh, yashavanth sinha, uma bharti or shatrughna sinha samet anya kai netaaon ne bhi goa kii baithak main shirkat nahin kii

 '' agle kareeb ek yaa dedh maheene kebhitar bhartiya cricket control board saal 2017-18 ke liye teenon grad (e, bi, si) main shaamil kiye jane vaale khilaadiyon ke naamon kaa elaan kar degaa
 It is expected that this time the board is going to give huge annual salary to the players
 isi mudde par kuch din pehle hi captain viraat kohli ne coach ravi shastri va mahendra singh dhoni ko saath lekar prashaskeey samiti ke chairman vinod raay se mulaakaat kii thi
 If sources are to be believed, the board has agreed to the demand of the players
 baavjood iske bahut hi bada gambhir sawaal uth rahaa he
 However, no matter how much the salaries of the board players increase, the truth is that they are miles away from their 'real and rightful pay'
 agar vastav main board apane samvidhan kii shartonke hisaab se khilaadiyon ko vetan de, to e grad main shaamil prayek khilaadi kaa salanaa vetan aasaani se kam se kam pachchis karod rupee to banataa hi he
 According to its constitution, the BCCI gives 70 per cent of the total annual revenue to domestic state units and 26 per cent of it to the players
 is 26 main se 13 fisadi international cricketron or 10
 The 6 share goes to domestic cricketers
 yah bhi padhein :matheus ke die 'gam vishesh' kaa 'kuch aise' badla liya viraat kohli ne! About 2 left there
 4 fisadi rajasav junior cricketron or mahila khilaadiyon ko diya jaataa he
 Of this thirty, the remaining four percent of the revenue goes towards the construction, maintenance and administrative expenses of stadiums
 is formule ko purv bisisiai adhyaksh jagmohan daalamia ne saal 2004 main purv cricketron anil kumble or rahul dravid se baatcheet ke baad hi hari jhandi dikhaai thi
 But after the IPL started in the year 2008, the attitude of the players changed as well
 vahiin haal hi main ipel ke chaar saal ke kareeb 16,000 karod rupee main bike prasaaran adhikaar ke baad khilaadiyon kii soch apane hisse ko lekar dhire-dhire or aakraamak or mukhar ho chali he
 But the board has in the past been playing its own game about salary
 bataa den ki khilaadiyon ko die jane vaala salanaa vetan kul rajasav ke duusare hisse30 fisadi (pehla hissaa 70 fisadi) main se diya jaataa he, board ke kul, yaa 100 fisadi rajasav main nahin
 At the same time, the most important thing is that the board does not include this 26 per cent of the revenue earned from Team India's international matches media, or broadcast rights (TV, Internet and mobile)
 jabaki board ko sabase zyada kamai hi prasaaran adhikaron se hoti he
 In such a situation, it seems like the dream of including the money received from the sale of broadcast rights of IPL to the players
 yah bhi padhein :isiilie viraat kohli darate hai pujaara ke saath 'kuch bhi' khilne se! At the same time, players also get a very small share from the sponsorship rights and the money received from ICC competitions
 lekin ab ab viraat and company chaahati he ki khilaadiyon ko board ko prasaaran adhikaron se hone vaali moti kamai se bhi hissaa mili
 Means both the broadcast rights of the Indian team and the broadcast rights of the IPL
 dhyaan dilaa den ki team india ke international match or ipel donon ke hi prasaaran adhikaar star sports ke paas hai
 Star Sports had paid around Rs 37,00 crore for media rights (TV, Internet and Mobile) from July 2012 to March 2018 of the Indian team's matches
 isse ek antarrashtriya match bisisiai ke liye ausat 40 karod rupee lekar aata he
 This means that every year only with the broadcasting rights of Team India, the BCCI got about six hundred and fifty million rupee aate hai
 26 per cent of this amount is about Rs 160 crore
 is rakam kaa international khilaadiyon par kharch 13 per cent to be done, that is eighty crores
 ab aap khud hi sochie ki agar sirf yahi 80 karod rupee international khilaadiyon ko salanaa mil jaaen, to har khilaadi ke hisse main kitni zyada rakam aegi
 At the same time, you can imagine that when BCCI is not sharing the share of these broadcasting rights with the players, how will it show the big heart of sharing the huge amount of 16,000 crore rupees from the IPL broadcast rights with the players
 aap dekhie ki 16000 karod kaa 26 fisadi 4160 karod rupee baithta he
 The comments yah bhi padhein :duusare din viraat kohli ne phenkaa record kaa 'satta' According to the BCCI constitution, if the amount of the right of the players is converted into annual income, then it is about Rs 832 crores (for international + domestic cricketers)
 is rakam kaa matlab yah he ki is salanaa 26 fisadi kaa 13 fisadi matlab team india ke khilaadiyon par kharch kii jane vaali rakam 416 karod rupee ho jaati he

 How much black money do Indians have in Swiss banks? This question is being raised in the country for the last several decades and often the politics of the country also starts revolving around this question
 ab khudaswiss bainkonki taraf se iskaa khulaayaa kiya he
 Data from the central bank of Switzerland has shown that the deposits of Indians in Swiss banks have almost halved to four and a half thousand crores
 swiss bainkon main videshiyon kaa kul 96 lakh karod rupee jamaa he jinamein se bharatiyon ke sirf saadhe chaar hajaar karod rupee he
 The amount deposited by Indians in these banks fell by about 45 per cent in 2016, which is the biggest decline in any one year
 2007 tak swiss bainkon main bharatiyon dwaara jamaa karai gai rakam arabon-kharbon main hua karti thi lekin uske baad blike mani par lagaam lagane kii koshishon kaa asar ye hua kikale dhanke kuberon ko swiss bainkon main paisa jamaa karnaa surakshit nahin lagane laga

 On March 19 this year, the Enforcement Directorate caught Tommy Patel and a few others while betting at a form house in Vadodara
 inaki giraftaar ke baad idi ko samaj main aayaa ki sattebaazi ke ek international racket kaa ek sargana unke haath aa gaya he
 Tommy Patel is a resident of Unjha in Gujarat, but he was running his business from Ahmedabad and Vadodara
 idi ko isi form house main kai mobile mili, saath hi airtel, tata ski or san tivi ke dicoder antina bhi, jinamein bina vigyaapan cricket match live aate the
 These decoders were provided to him by someone named Sanjay from Delhi
 yaheen se match dekhte hue log mobile ke jariye sattebaazi kaa kaarobaar chalaaya karte the
 Enforcement Directorate counsel Rajesh Kanani told us that all these bookies used to do full business in coded language even on mobile phones
 yah puraa kaarobaar mobile ke zariye hota tha
 All these bookies were connected live on number one
 baahar ke buki apana number silent (mut) par rakhte or har 10 over ke baad unki taraf se satte kii ghoshnaa hoti
 On this basis, every bookie would write his own dialect
 ye puri baatcheet record hoti or isi aadhaar par baad main len-dein hota
 There is a code for every bookie, and this is the code that these people talk to each other
 idi ne jaanch main ye bhi dekha ki ye log britain kii company betfere
 The laws of the com were also using illegitimate
 betfere dot com main ek super master log-in idi milti he, jisamen qareeb 3 lakh america dollar pehle se jamaa karaane hote hai taaki aap kam se kam utani rakam kaa satta khel saken
 To take advantage of this, Tommy Patel enlisted the help of Delhi hawala businessman Mukesh Kumar alias Mukesh Delhi
 mukesh sharma dilli sthit hawala kaarobaari tha
 He had Punt Master login-ids
 mukesh ne hawala ke jariye england main rah rahe sukhminder singh lodhi ko paise bhejkar ek super master log-in idi khulwaayi thi
 10 Master Log-in ids are opened under one Super Master ID, which is given to individual bookies
 har master log-in idi ke tahat 30-30 customer log-in idi ho sakate hai
 That is, 300 people can bet under one master log-in ID
 aise mukesh sharma hi akelaa 1500 logon kii betting karwaata tha
 The ED came to know that in the last 3 years, Mukesh Sharma transferred more than 50 crore rupees through hawala to Sodhi, the money coming and going through hawala is not visible in anyone's bank account
 isi tarah karodon kaa kaarobaar chalata rahaa
 The question is whether there is any formula between Tommy Patel and IPL betting
 yahaan ritesh bansal urf bharat dilli kaa zikr aata he, jo tommy patel ke saath sattebaazi main shaamil tha

 yahaan ke kaarobaar main tommy patel ke saath ritesh bansal urf bharat dilli bhi shaamil tha
 The comments yahi nahin, tommy patel dubai ke buki dilip sindhi or pakistan-karachi ke buki gulambhai se bhi judaa hua he
 That is, these wires spread around the world of betting are found in many places among themselves
 ab tak is maamle main saat log pakade gaye hai, lekin chaar aaropee ab tak giraft se baahar hai

 ye dicoder inhen dilli se sanjay naam ke kisi shaks ne muhaiyaa karaae the

 All this business was done through mobile
 ye sabhi buki ek-ek number par live jude hote the
 Outside bookies put their number on silent (mute) and after every 10 overs, betting would be announced from their side
 is aadhaar par har buki apni boli likhva detaa

 har buki ke liye ek code hota he or isi code se ye log aapas main baat karte hai

 com ke kaayadon kaa bhi nazaij istemaal kar rahe the

com has a Super Master Login ID, which requires depositing close to 3 lakh US dollars in advance so that you can bet at least that much amount

 yani ek master log-in idi ke tahat 300 log betting kar sakate hai

 (input bhashaa se) Jyotindra Jain At the end of the nineteenth century when the technologies of mass production of visual image (such as lithography) arrived in India, nationalist uplift and independence movement was also emerging in the country
 tasveeron ke vyapak prasar kaa phayda swatantraaa andolan ke vichaaron or sandeshon ko vyapak str par failaane main mila
 The depiction of contexts and reality gave colonial lessons the traditionally flat and idealized imagination endowed with more tangible figures, which immediately attracted the masses
 iske alaava, 1850 ke dashak se bharat main photography kaa aagaman—rashtravaadi netaaon ko drishy pahchaan or aradhy sareekha sthaan pradaan karne ke liye kalakaaron ke jariye niojit yathartwaadee chithran kii shakti ke saath-saath puure bharat main aam janata ke bich swatantraaa ke liye bade paimaane par junun or utsaah kaa sanchaar hua
 a plethora of popular images of Mahatma Gandhi — including photographs of his personal life as well as cinematography of all aspects of his leadership of the independence movement — became the subject of his popular image-making, which distinguished him like a mythological deity
 19veen shatabdi ke ant or 20veen shatabdi kii shuruyaat main sabase prasiddh lithographic preson main kalakatta sthit chor bagan art studio or kalakatta art studio shaamil the; puna sthit chitrashaala press; bombai—or uske baad kurlaa-lonawala sthit ravi verma press or kuch had tak baad kii avadhi main shuru hua mathura kaa brijbasi press jisaki kai or sthanon par shakhaaen bhi thim

 inke alaava, kai chote or kshetreey litho press puure bharat main khul rahe the jo saste poster, calendar, utpaadon ke label or anya prachaar saamagree bana rahe the or jisane drishy chhavi ko aam aadmi ke haathon tak pahunchaaya jo pehle kabhi nahin hua tha

 This law will replace the two-decade-old system of appointment of judges in the Supreme Court and High Courts

The court said that you are saying that the data is with the District Election Officer, but why have you not got the data after 3 years? On behalf of the Election Commission, it was said that the data is with the District Election Officer and three weeks' time is required so that the data can be called

 The Lok Prahari had filed a petition in the Supreme Court asking that the Supreme Court order the election reforms, that at the time of nomination, the candidate should also disclose the source of income of himself and the family
 ise lekar supreme court ne centre sarkaar or chunaav ayog ko notice jari kar jawaab maanga tha
 In its affidavit in April 2017, the Center had said in the Supreme Court about the election reforms that at the time of nomination, the Center is ready to make necessary information about the source of income of the candidate, his life partner and dependents
 centre ne kaha ki kaaphi vichaar karne ke baad is mudde par niyamon main badlaav kaa faisla liya gaya he
 Notification for this will be released soon
 isse pehle chunaav ayog bhi is maamle main apni sahmati jataa chukaa he
 The comments chunaav ayog ne kaha tha ki swasth loktantr ke liye niyamon main ye badlaav jaruri he
 According to the rules so far, the candidate is required to give information about his, spouse and three dependents' movable-immovable property and liabilities at the time of nomination, but there is no rule in this about the source of income
 isi ko lekar NGO lokprahari ne supreme court main yachika daakhil kar kaha tha ki supreme court chunaav sudhaaron ko lekar aadesh de ki namakan ke vakt pratyaashee apni or parivaar kii aay ke strot kaa khulaasa bhi kare
